                c:IDA ?= this
                AND = {
                    c:JOD ?= this
                    NOT = { exists = c:IDA }
                }
                AND = {
                    NOR = {
                        exists = c:JOD
                        exists = c:IDA
                    }
                    c:BIC ?= this
                }
            }
        }
        interest_group_trigger = {
            ig_counts_as_marginal = no
            is_interest_group_type = ig_armed_forces
        }
        earliest_usage_date = 1878.1.1 # joined the Jodhpur risala/cavalry
        latest_usage_date = 1902.8.9 # promoted to Major-General

    }
    commander_usage = {

                        exists = c:JOD
                        exists = c:IDA
                    }
                    c:BIC ?= this
                }

						state_region = s:STATE_SANTIAGO
					}
				}
				AND = {
					c:PLT ?= THIS
					country_has_primary_culture = cu:south_andean

						state_region = s:STATE_SANTIAGO
					}
				}
			}

	last_name = Balmaceda
	historical = yes
	female = no
	role = character_role_politician
	culture = primary_culture
	religion = rel:catholic
	interest_group = ig_intelligentsia
	ideology = ideology_reformer
    home_region = STATE_SANTIAGO
	birth_date = 1840.7.19
	traits = {
		imperious
		experienced_diplomat
	}
    interest_group_leader_usage = {
        country_trigger = {
			OR = {
				c:CHL ?= THIS
				AND = {
					c:FND ?= THIS
					any_scope_state = {
						state_region = s:STATE_SANTIAGO
					}
				}
				AND = {
					c:PLT ?= THIS
					country_has_primary_culture = cu:south_andean
					any_scope_state = {
						state_region = s:STATE_SANTIAGO
					}
				}
			}
			has_dlc_feature = rp1_content
        }
        interest_group_trigger = {
			is_interest_group_type = ig_intelligentsia
        }
        earliest_usage_date = 1878.1.1
        latest_usage_date = 1895.1.1
        #guaranteed to spawn if possible
    }
	trait_generation = { }
}

			}

					}

					c:PLT ?= THIS

						state_region = s:STATE_SANTIAGO
					}

    ideology = ideology_sovereignist_leader
    home_region = STATE_EASTERN_CUBA
    traits = {
        persistent
        brave
        honorable
        social_bandit
    }
    agitator_usage = {
        country_trigger = {
            c:CUB ?= this
            has_dlc_feature = ip4_content
        }
        interest_group_trigger = {
            is_interest_group_type = ig_rural_folk
        }
        earliest_usage_date = 1868.10.10 # start of the Ten Years' War
        latest_usage_date = 1895.1.1
        #guaranteed to spawn if possible
    }
    commander_usage = {
        country_trigger = {
            c:CUB ?= this
            OR = {
                is_subject = no
                AND = {
                    is_subject = yes
                    liberty_desire > 50
                }
            }
            has_dlc_feature = ip4_content
        }
        role = general
        earliest_usage_date = 1874.1.1
        latest_usage_date = 1895.1.1
        #guaranteed to spawn if possible
    }
    on_created = {
        if = {
            limit = {
                home_country ?= {
                    is_subject = no
                }
            }
            set_ideology = ideology:ideology_radical # Dios, la Razón y la Virtud
        }
    }
}

				is_subject = yes
			}
			has_dlc_feature = rp1_content
		}

    }

        if = {
            limit = {
                owner ?= {
                    has_technology_researched = corporatism
                }
            }
            set_ideology = ideology:ideology_miguelist_2
        }
    }
}

	ideology = ideology_carlist
	birth_date = 1855.6.25
	home_region = STATE_CATALONIA
	traits = {
		pious
		reserved
		basic_political_operator
	}
    interest_group_leader_usage = {
        country_trigger = {
        	OR = {
        		c:SPA ?= this
        		country_has_primary_culture = cu:catalan
        	}
			any_scope_state = {
				state_region = s:STATE_CATALONIA
			}
			has_dlc_feature = ip4_content
        }
        interest_group_trigger = {
			is_interest_group_type = ig_landowners
        }
        earliest_usage_date = 1875.1.1
        latest_usage_date = 1901.12.31
        #guaranteed to spawn if possible
    }
	trait_generation = { }
	on_created = {
        if = {
            limit = {
                owner ?= {
                    has_technology_researched = corporatism
                }
            }
            set_ideology = ideology:ideology_carlist_2
        }
	}
}

        set_variable = house_bourbon
		set_variable = legitimist_leader
        if = {
            limit = {
                owner ?= {
                    has_technology_researched = corporatism
                }
            }
            set_ideology = ideology:ideology_carlist_2
        }
    }
}

    first_name = Abraham
    last_name = Lincoln
    historical = yes
    culture = cu:yankee
    female = no
    religion = rel:protestant
    ideology = ideology_abolitionist
    interest_group = ig_petty_bourgeoisie
    birth_date = 1809.2.12
    dna = dna_abraham_lincoln
	home_region = STATE_ILLINOIS
    traits = {
        experienced_political_operator
        inspirational_orator
        tactful
    }
    interest_group_leader_usage = {
        country_trigger = {
            exists = c:USA
            c:USA ?= THIS
            NOT = {
                has_global_variable = ruler_selector_abraham_lincoln
            }
        }
        interest_group_trigger = {
            ig_counts_as_marginal = no
            OR = {
                is_interest_group_type = ig_petty_bourgeoisie
                is_interest_group_type = ig_intelligentsia
            }
            NOR = {
				has_variable = communist_ig_var
				has_variable = chose_vanguardism
				has_variable = chose_fascism
				has_variable = chose_conservatism
				has_variable = chose_ethno_nationalism
			}
        }
        earliest_usage_date = 1844.2.12
        latest_usage_date = 1890.1.1
        #guaranteed to spawn if possible
    }
}
